The reason we look youthful in our younger years and start to look like shit in our older years is directly related to how quickly our cells are replicating. Take your skin for example. When you're young, when your skin cells start to die, new ones replace them. So it always looks bright and youthful. When you get older, your cells aren't replicating as quickly. So the old dead cells are the ones that are sitting there. That's why it starts to wrinkle and look like shit. The reason our cells stop replicating is because they have run out of length on their telomeres. Telemeres are the little caps at the end of our chromosomes. Every time our cells divide and replicate themselves, those caps get a little bit shorter. Once they get so short that you can't use them anymore, the cell dies. That's what aging is. Epitale on is heavily researched and shown to increase the length of our telomeres. In essence, giving us the ability to stay youthful and produce new cells for a longer time. The reason we look youthful in our younger years and start to look like shit in our older years is directly related to how quickly our cells are replicating. Take your skin for example. When you're young, when your skin cells start to die, new ones replace them. So it always looks bright and youthful. When you get older, your cells aren't replicating as quickly. So the old dead cells are the ones that are sitting there. That's why it starts to wrinkle and look like shit. The reason our cells stop replicating is because they have run out of length on their telomeres. Telemeres are the little caps at the end of our chromosomes. Every time our cells divide and replicate themselves, those caps get a little bit shorter. Once they get so short that you can't use them anymore, the cell dies. That's what aging is. Epitale on is heavily researched and shown to increase the length of our telomeres. In essence, giving us the ability to stay youthful and produce new cells for a longer time. And when the cell can't divide, it dies, and that's what causes aging. The reason number one is if you grew up in a strict household, always have it a walk on eggshells. You were trained from birth that anything easy or calm is unsafe. Number two is nice, doesn't spike a dopamine. Kindness feels flat, and everybody's so overstimulated that the chase of validation is a way better high. And lastly, your brain confuses familiarity for chemistry. You've only ever been in a relationship where you're the one who's more interested. Unless you disrupt that pattern, you're gonna end up in the same exact cycle over it. If this hits a little too close to home, you're not cooked, you're just used to be an on fire. Disrupt the pattern.

Two years ago I gave up a multiple six figure income, which could have led to a million dollar income if I had kept going, but I gave all that up to go start a business with my partner because there's something I cared about more. But that can happen at any time in your life. And if you're not on a path where you're already making great money, then what do you have to lose? The only thing that's stopping you is this idea in your head that you've got one direction in life and that's the only one that you can follow. But you can do this at any time in your life. There are guys who don't reinvent their lives until they're in their 40s and 50s. So if you're someone who feels like you're on the wrong path but you're already in your 20s or 30s, take the leap of faith and try it. ## If you don’t have a mentor that has what you want go find one 
URL: https://www.tiktok.com/@jacobnach/video/7512496953649941791

This is how doing the exact opposite of every successful person's advice grew my business to over six figures a month. Because here's the trap. You go ask a guy who's working 80 hours a week at a job he hates, but he's making great money. And you ask that guy how to make money. What do you think he's going to tell you? Go work a job you hate for 80 hours a week. And if that's what you want to do, then that's fine. But if you're someone who says, I want to work 20 hours a week, still make great money, have time for a family and having a life, then that's not the guy to talk to. And here's the crazy part. Some of you guys are idolizing these people that are miserable. I don't know about you guys, but at least for me, my goal is not to be miserable. Just because someone makes more money than you do doesn't mean they have better advice. Start taking advice only from people that you would trade lives with right now and watch how fast you start moving towards your goals and not further away.
